At that time, we wanted a room on a higher floor. When we arrived, we were upgraded to a room with a bathtub for free, and the drinks in the room mini bar were free. The service was very good and considerate. When we left the hotel, we were asked about our stay. The air conditioning temperature control was not good, the temperature could not be lowered, and it was a bit hot. There was a noise in the bathroom in the middle of the night. I contacted the waiter. It turned out to be a sound insulation problem. The next door guest was using a hair dryer. I was a little disappointed.
The hotel is directly connected to the business, and Wanbao City is opposite. It is very convenient to eat takeout. The takeout is delivered to the hotel by a robot.
Our package includes a Chinese meal, which is enough for a family of three. The dishes are relatively exquisite. There are not too many varieties of breakfast.
Convenient to travel, there is a subway station at the door of the hotel, and it is convenient to go to downtown Hangzhou. Overall, it is not bad, and I will choose to stay here in the future.

msg:酒店環境還可以，也乾淨整潔，服務沒有五星級的標準。我們入住三晚，第一天自助早餐，後面接到酒店電話説因為考慮到近期疫情比較嚴重，所以採用早餐送房，門口放個椅子。第一天送餐，一碗稀飯，2個沙糖桔，2個小饅頭，1個小油條，1個雞蛋，一份蘆筍炒蝦仁（幾乎沒味道），沒有任何下飯的，後來打電話反映送了一包榨菜。第二天等到9:30都沒送，結果打電話去，前台説忘記了，然後等了20分鐘送上來如下圖的東西，都是已經冷了，這次連個粥都沒了。後來電話去讓送碗麪，結果是清湯麪加兩片青菜。醉了，128元的早餐啊。我們可以理解酒店送餐服務，也覺得挺好的。但這餐食也太差勁了👎。另外電話過去，前台都是冷冰冰的語氣，都是詢問也沒反饋，每次都是再打電話去反饋結果。超級被動！整體服務差勁，根本不符合五星級的標準。我基本不寫評論，但這次真心被氣到了！
